<Review>My husband's grandmother was a parishioner of this church most of her 100.5 years she graced this earth.

She passed in the time of COVID, requiring a change to our traditional Catholic services.
The church handled her services BEAUTIFULLY. Father spoke of such joy and how her many years gives us examples of Gods love and why we are here. We left with love and joy in our hearts saying "for now" to our grandmother until we can be united again.

Thank you for giving my husband light in his hurting during this loss. He has spoken many times since how much better he felt after listen to her service. I was very impressed with Father Tony, he is doing the work our Father put him here to do.</Review><userid>104375207726545793734</userid>< pictures>

<Time>1612757599934<//Time>< Review>
I just went. I NEVER write reviews but this deserves one. So to began with servers need to be pay better or have a real talk because their attitude is HORRIBLE they treat you as if you are getting food for free. Not only that but it took 30min for me to get my tacos with only two customers ahead of me. I was wondering why with other workers being there and two more stations (closed) they couldn't go faster. Well to make things worse, the owners got there with about 7 people AND THEN they open a second station just to serve them. Owners didn't care about their customers, how long they had being waiting there or the service they were getting. They just proceed to skip the line and order for all family members. Also they way their tacos were serve compare to mine was very different, I got very little meat compare to them. But whatever, let's talk about the guacamole and how brow it was, also the attitude of the taquero when I asked for fresh guac to the guy. He made faces and also since I asked for toppings of the side he gave me onion, cilantro and guac ONLY when I was suppose to get tomato sauce too. When I asked for it he said he didn't have containers for it... while at the register there was a guy packing salsa to go. Tacos are no great or even good, customer service is HORRIBLE and experiencing the entitlement of the owners encourage me to write this. DO NOT COME HERE!!!!

And remember if they give you yellow lemons and limit the amount of salsa you take they are NOT legit tacos.< /Review>

< Text>
SABA is a shia muslim Islamic center where we the goal of the center is to promote the message of Islam and to facilitate its practice according to the Jafri school of thought. At a given time in special months like Ramadan or Muharram SABA has 4 programs in parallel. Arabic, Persian, English and Urdu. There is food (Tabarruk) served after every program. Also it has SABA Rise academy which is a accredited school upto 8th grade. They have toddlers and TK classes as well.< /Text>

I love this place!

I've been eating at this location a lot since this past summer and I've never had a bad experience.

The manager here is always super helpful and always goes above and beyond to make sure I've had a pleasant dining experience.

But all the employees are friendly.

Considering the prices are relatively low the food is really good and I appreciate all their healthy selections, especially the spinach wraps.

The app is also easy to use and it pays to use it to order ahead since sometimes they can get really busy here.

It's definitely turned into one if my favorite low-key places to eat.< /Review>

<text>The name might suggest that this is primarily a burger joint and way way back when, it was. These days they still have some great burgers and an amazing chicken club sandwich along with onion rings and French fries. They have also added an extensive Mexican food menu as well. These guys know how to make some great Mexican dishes quickly too. There is only outdoor seating here but that area is covered to keep the rain off of you on those rare days that it rains in Southern California. Wear a jacket if it is chilly outside though because you will not be indoors at any time here. There is a walk up window where you place your order and another window where you will pick up your order once it is ready. Nothing here is prepared in advance. Your order is freshly cooked once you place it but these guys have mastered the art of quickly preparing any of their menu items so you won't be waiting too long for your food. The small wait is very much worth it. These are freshly made dishes done quickly but done right. I highly recommend their fish tacos or chicken club sandwich. Their chili cheese fries with freshly diced onions is a meal in itself and is a wonderful hangover cure. I quite honestly have never had anything from their menu that I did not like. There are also enough different choices that there is going to be something that will make your mouth and stomach happy you stopped by.< /text>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<date>1447191545222<//date><Review>I ended up looking for a new car unexpectedly when my car was totaled in an accident. I spent a few days researching online, and a few days going to different dealerships. Auto City was out of the way of most of the ones I went to, and I am so glad I made the time to go. The first difference between Auto City and all of the other dealerships I went was that neither Victor (who helped me on my first visit) nor Fraser (who helped me on my second and third visits) tried to rush me into a decision. Every other dealership was more concerned with how quickly they could sell me a car than they were with ensuring that I was going to be satisfied with my purchase. For example, one dealership insisted that I test drive only the car I felt the most like purchasing to streamline the process. At Auto City, I test drove six cars before I could decide which one I was happiest with, and Fraser was patient and happy to offer up tips and information about the cars I drove. Both Victor and Fraser were very knowledgeable about the vehicles I asked about. When it came down to purchasing my vehicle, Fraser helped me get a great loan - one even better than my own bank was willing to give me.

On top of everything else, I found more high-quality used vehicles within my price range at Auto City than I did anywhere else. Their vehicles were all cleaned, inside and out, and shined like they had been waxed even though it rained almost every day that week. It was clear that Auto City cares equally about the state of their vehicles and their customer's happiness - quite a lot. < Review>
I purchased my car from this dealership for one reason, they had an onsite service facility. When I picked the car I liked from the lot and took it for a test drive it had acceleration issues. I was already hooked on wanting the car, so I trusted the service dept to fix the issue. It took them a day to fix which was a but aggravating but I fell in love with the car and wanted it. Because of this issue, the service tech was a standup guy who I felt I could trust, and the fact I know nothing about Acuras; I purchased the $2500 service plan. The reason I’m giving this place two stars is the $2500 I spent on the service plan is basically flushed down the toilet. It is impossible to get an appointment reasonably for car service. I’ve called nearly every four months for the past two years to get my car serviced here and every single time they tell me the schedule is full for two weeks. They won’t offer any alternative like calling you if a cancellation happens and you’re able to be squeezed in. they tell me if my car isn’t running or is in need of immediate service I can drop it off and a service technician can take a look at it when they get around to it or by the time my appointment is scheduled (which is two weeks). So essentially I’m dropping my car off and getting a rental car until their service technician can take a look at it hopefully within the next two weeks; which is ludicrous. i’ve also called a number of times to get clarification on my service plan to see if a part is covered under the plan like a starter. they don’t have any information on the service plan that you purchased; you have to call the service plan 800 number. So while my experience purchasing the car at this dealership was OK the after care and the interactions with the service department have been absolutely miserable.<//Review>

< text>
I bought exceptionally good 2016 Honda Odyssey in Auto City. I was assured that the car has no issues and when I took it to an official dealership 3 days later they confirmed that there is nothing to do with the car and it's in a perfect condition.

The staff there is so easy to communicate with, they behave like your friends and don't push hard on you. They did push a little on their extended warranty, so I had to listen for 20 minutes what it is and why I need it even though I previously said I don't need it, but it does not compare with the pressure in any official dealership, where they try to squeeze every single dollar out of you.

Financial department there does need some improvement, because they are not willing to get you the lowest rate possible. Initially they gave me 5.99% interest rate with my Excellent credit score, I asked them to search better and in a minute they found 4.99%. I expected it to be around 4.0% or less, but they said there is nothing better. When I signed the contract I found out that the financial company is "Auto City Sales", not a bank or credit union, so they were extremely interested to keep the interest rate as high as possible, because it's their direct profit. Anyways, it's not a big deal.

I like their website and high quality photos of the cars, free CarFax reports. The price you see there is what you will actually pay if you decline their extended warranty and KARR security system.

Overall, I like my experience with Auto City very much. My personal recommendation goes to Alex - ask for him, he's really willing to find you the car you want for the price you need.< /text>

Jose is not the ordinary car salesman you would think of. Secondly, Jose keeps in touch with you to see how things are going and he also remembers what your interests are in a vehicle while at the same time giving you options with the vehicles that the dealership has. I can assure you that if you want to look at cars freely, not lied to for the sake of a sale, but to be heard of what your needs are then Jose Martinez and Auto City Sales is the one you would want to visit.

Thirdly, I am a first time car buyer and I came in knowing of what car salesman try to do. I came in after I had done my research and quite honestly I did not encounter anything negative with Jose at all. <Review>My husband and I were in the market for a used car this past winter. We were driving around dealerships in East County and drove past Auto City. We were impressed by the strong reviews on Google and Yelp, so we stopped in.

We were introduced to Alfred and we shared the characteristics we were looking for in a car. He explained to us that the car specifications are primarily online (vs. posted on vehicles in the lot), and essentially handed over his computer for us to view the inventory online. He didn't hover or pressure us - which we really appreciated. We found a car we liked and asked to test drive. We got the keys and were told to be back in an hour. We LOVED the car, but it was two days before Christmas and we were nervous about the timing. We were considering getting the car checked out by a mechanic before purchasing, so we were concerned about buying right before the holidays. Alfred showed us how to put a hold on the vehicle, so we were able to come back on the 26th.

When we arrived on the 26th, we were greeted with excellent customer service once again. We were provided with the keys to get the car checked out by a mechanic. There were no issues with the vehicle. We financed the car with SDCCU (because the rates were a bit better) and we did not get pressured by Auto City to change our decision.

When we returned to Auto City to purchase the car and finalize the paperwork, everyone was extremely friendly and efficient. The whole process only took a couple of hours and was nearly stress-free - we haven't been able to say that about any other car buying experience.

As an extra bonus, we noticed the car didn't have floor mats. Alfred told us to stay in touch with him and to reach out if we saw a similar car on the website in the inventory moving forward. We did, reached out to Albert, and he gave us the floor mats of that similar vehicle without charge.

We love our new car and had a great experience. Overall, I highly recommend considering Auto City if you're in the market for a used vehicle!<//Review></record>

< Review>
My wife and I were looking for a used car several months ago.  We stopped at Kia of El Cajon to check out a lease special they had and left feeling the particular icky feeling you have after you leave most car dealerships.  On our way out, we saw the sign for Auto City, which is just down the street, and decided to go there.

We were not immediately rushed upon by a gaggle of sales people, like most dealerships.  Instead, we were greeted by Alfred.  He explained to us that the easiest way to look through their inventory was to look through their website at a computer in their office.  We went in and told him what we were looking for and he pulled up a list of all the vehicles that matched our criteria.  There were no attempts to up-sell us to a more expensive vehicle.  He was also realistic and up front about what financing options we had and what our monthly payments would be.

After he filtered their inventory to match our criteria, he left us at his desk to look through what was available.  Occasionally, he would stop in to see if we had questions.  Once we chose the vehicle we were interested in, we let him know and he got it out for us to test drive.

By the time we were done test driving, it was late and we wanted to think about the car before buying it so Alfred let us know we could put a hold on the car for a couple of days, which we ended up doing.

We came back two days later to test drive again, as well as take the car to a mechanic to be inspected.  Upon a good report from the mechanic, we decided to buy.  We let Alfred know and he got the process rolling with paperwork, signatures, etc.  We went to our own bank for financing and it was a pretty smooth process.

All in all, we were able to test drive and purchase a car within the the span of a couple of hours.  The was very little pressure.  In fact, the only upsell attempt came at the financing desk where they tried to offer us additional warranties, paint coating, and other classic car dealership add-ons.  Once the pitch was over, we said no and they moved on.  It was nice and simple.

I would definitely recommend checking out Auto City for used cars.  The people were friendly and low pressure.  There's no negotiating for prices (prices are comparatively low already).  And they have a 6 month warranty that's included, which is nice.  If you're looking for a car, check them out!<//Review>

< Text>
My experience at AutoCity was okay. I got a car fairly quickly. Took 1 day. But the hype and the high reviews about this place  are a little misleading. Perhaps it’s my fault for not doing my research enough.
Anyway, why 3 stars? Well I got what came for, so really no less. It could have been worse. Why not higher? Well, they advertise fair prices, high quality inspections to ensure the cars are well maintained before you buy them, and non-pushy, relaxed sales tactics. However, I was constantly rushed and pushed to buy the car quickly, being told that the cars don’t last long, and that someone else was coming to look at the car later. I realize those may be true, but it’s not really following true to the company “vision” or whatever. I was also pressured to make this review several times. Just leave me alone please! If it’s not pertaining to the car and my purchase, please stop harassing me.
As far as fair prices/quality of of the vehicle, it seems okay. I’m a little concerned because the vehicle, despite having a decent engine, starts to struggle around 65 mph, which the salesman told me was normal for those cars...but it’s not. Also, the S belt started acting up right away. There are a couple of cracks on the wind shield despite having “no damage”. The vehicle exterior was dirty. Part of the interior- I don’t even know what it is...it looks like an iPod holder or something, is broken and can come right out.
It’s these little things that really add up to a less-than-stellar experience. I wish my salesman was more knowledgeable and less pushy (considering the company views). I wish the car was in a more “prepared” state when I bought it.
There is a 3 day return policy, so I could have returned it. And I considered it, but I opted against it.
A positive thing they do is take care of all the DMV issues. So that’s nice. I would have preferred to write this review after I received the registration/title in the mail as it takes a few weeks, but I’m writing early in the hopes that my sales agent will stop asking me to write one.

TL:DR
Nice place if you know exactly what you want and what you will pay for it.
Not the best experience otherwise due to misleading advertising.<//Text>

<user_name>Ted Torre-Bueno<//user_name><Date>1376524566747<//Date><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
My wife and I bought a used Prius at Auto City Sales six weeks ago and enough time has now gone by that I know I made the right decision buying the car from them. I've had it checked out by the service department at Kearney Mesa Toyota and the car is exactly what they Stan told me it was - a great buy in great shape.

After having a really unfortunate experience trying to buy a used vehicle at San Diego Toyota I started doing a lot of research and found out that many auto dealers, new and used, have terrible Yelp ratings. I finally found Auto City Sales by the time I was simultaneously talking to half a dozen dealers, and I actually found out that the fact that they have a good Yelp rating really did set them apart.

Stan was always honest, polite, thorough, and informative. I run my own company, and didn't have a lot of time to buy a car, so I really valued that he gave me simple, short, direct answers. There was no negotiating or BS - they had the car I wanted, it was a great price, it was exactly what they said it was. I came by, test drove the car, did all the paperwork and was in and out in less than an hour. I'm only in my late thirties, so I've probably bought less than a dozen cars in my life, but this was by far the best, and fastest experience I've ever had with buying a car.

Now I'm recommending them to my wife's folks (and I like my wife's folks) and whoever else I know that is buying a new car. I even recommended them to one of the service technicians over at Toyota of San Diego!

I've read some of the negative reviews that these guys have gotten, and I notice that what those people really seem upset about is the fact that the Auto City folks don't haggle. I think that's pretty short sighted because I looked up the KBB on the car I was buying and I know I got an amazing deal. Of course they don't haggle - they don't waste your time trying to sell you at an inflated price, they just give you the best price they can afford. I really appreciated that.

The other negative review I noticed said they were rude and evasive. That may have been their experience - I suspect they misread direct as rude, which would be  their loss because these guys were just about the only auto dealers I talked to who were scrupulously honest about everything from beginning to end.

Basically, I can't say enough good things about them. Thanks, Auto City.<//Review>

<text>The Good:

I would describe this dealership as the "Costco" of used cars. What I mean by that is, you get what you pay for and the price is fair. This is opposed to the haggling, bargaining, and hassle that goes into most other dealers.

The actual dealers are the most polite, friendly, and honest out off all the dealers I met when shopping for my current vehicle. Victor Gonzalez in particular who helped me pick out my 2012 Yaris was very honest and straightforward with any questions I had. He did not employ any shady tactics in trying to sell me the car and did not waste my time, if anything, he made the process as pain free as possible. He has a great sense of humor and seems like a great guy. He even gave me brand new floor mats which I didn't see until I had gotten home!

The Bad: If you come here expecting to haggle your way into a "steal of a deal" don't bother. Their prices are set for a reason and they don't like to waste time. But on the flip side, the vehicles did seem to be of good quality, well maintained, with detailed vehicle history reports.

The Ugly: The only things I found shady were their promise of a "Warranty" that really covers nothing. If it weren't for this, I would have easily given 5 stars. However, as soon as I inquired about it, they gave me the full details and let me know that it is a "buyer beware" situation. However, the risk is worth the fair price you will pay for the vehicle, because I do not believe that any of the vehicles they sell are lemons or junkers due to the extensive honesty with which they present the car history. Its no more risky than buying from a private seller, but only slightly less risky than a "certified" dealer.

Overall: I would recommend this place for friends and family. As long as you've had your coffee, know what the "warranty" is, and set aside a day to do your shopping, Auto City Sales in El Cajon will make the process as safe, stressless, and fun as possible!< /text>< name>
